<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реактивный.html>реакти́вный</a> (7357)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реактивный.html>реакти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reaktívnyj</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реакция.html>реа́кция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reákcija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реакция.html>реа́кции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реакция.html>реа́кции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реакция.html>реа́кций</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реализация.html>реализа́ция</a> (4927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализация.html>реализа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">realizácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализация.html>реализа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализация.html>реализа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализация.html>реализа́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>realization <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the act of making real</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***реализовывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реализовывать.html>реализо́вывать</a> (28454)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">realizovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовывать.html>реализо́вывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">realizóvyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реализовать.html>реализова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to implement, to carry out, to realize</li>
<li>to sell, to realize</li></ol>

***реанимация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ция</a> (15100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">reanimácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реанимация.html>реанима́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resuscitation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resuscitation department</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> resuscitation ambulance</li>
<li>revival, effort to breathe life</li></ol>

***ребенок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a> (174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">робя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">robja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminitive of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">робъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">robŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orbę</i>. Compare with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́робок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párobok</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>. The relationship with "slave" could arise from the meaning "orphan" because orphans carried out the hard work in the household.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rebjónok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́т</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребеночек.html>ребёночек</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Use the second plural with the meaning "friends!", "fellows!", "guys!", "comrades!".</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></span>, less commonly <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> child, kid, baby: children, kids, babies
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ditjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> guys, fellows, friends, comrades</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The singular form can only refer to "child"/"baby" sense.</li>
<li>The plural form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjáta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> can mean "guys", "friends", etc.</li>
<li>For the plural form "children" <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is the preferred word but <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjáta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also used.</li>
<li>The suppletive plural form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is originally a plural form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ditjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***ребячий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребячий.html>ребя́чий</a> (15013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rebjáta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with unexpected iotation (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щенячий.html>щеня́чий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ščenjáčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребячий.html>ребя́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rebjáčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> children's, child's</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> childish</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rebjónok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребя́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rebjáta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребятишки.html>ребяти́шки</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rebjatíški</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***реветь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реве́ть</a> (4085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Infinitive modified by analogy with 1sg. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реву́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">revú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рюти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*řuti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:реветь.html>реве́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">revétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взреветь.html>взреве́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зареветь.html>зареве́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прореветь.html>прореве́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roar, to bellow, to howl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cry, to weep (loudly)</li></ol>
